      <p>This is a list of cities and states sorted by the CIA-based inflation rate. <a href="/wiki/Inflation_rate" class="mw-redirect" title="Inflation rate">Inflation rate</a> is defined as the annual percent change in consumer prices compared with the previous year's consumer prices. </p>
      <p>The list is based on the <a href="/wiki/CIA_World_Factbook" class="mw-redirect" title="CIA World Factbook">CIA World Factbook</a> data<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> unless otherwise indicated, and is updated according to the statistical updates by respective cities. </p>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="List_of_countries_by_five-year_trend">List of countries by five-year trend</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_inflation_rate&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: List of countries by five-year trend">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>Countries are sorted by their inflation rate in 2017.
